identity: the identity that the policy decision applies to\n//   - policy: a string description of the policy being evaluated\n//   - verdict: the result of the policy evaluation (e.g., \"allow\", \"deny\")\n//   - reason: a string explaining why this verdict was reached\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy, verdict, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity,\n\t\t\"policy\":           policy,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          verdict,\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t})\n\n\tscopedLog.Log(pal.logLevel, \"Policy decision\")\n\n\t// Write to custom output if configured\n\tif pal.output != nil {\n\t\tauditEvent := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"type\":     \"policy_decision\",\n\t\t\t\"identity\": identity,\n\t\t\t\"policy\":   policy,\n\t\t\t\"verdict\":  verdict,\n\t\t\t\"reason\":   reason,\n\t\t}\n\t\tif data, err := json.Marshal(auditEvent); err == nil {\n\t\t\tpal.output.Write(append(data, '\\n'))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs the result of a policy evaluation.\n//\n// Parameters:\n//   - ctx: context for the evaluation\n//   - policyKey: key identifying the policy being evaluated\n//   - selectorCache: the SelectorCache used during evaluation\n//   - result: the result of the policy evaluation\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey string, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result interface{}) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyKey: policyKey,\n\t\t\"evaluation\":        \"complete\",\n\t})\n\n\tscopedLog.Log(pal.logLevel, \"Policy evaluation completed\")\n\n\t// Write to custom output if configured\n\tif pal.output != nil {\n\t\tauditEvent := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"type\":       \"policy_evaluation\",\n\t\t\t\"policyKey\":  policyKey,\n\t\t\t\"result\":     result,\n\t\t\t\"hasCache\":   selectorCache != nil,\n\t\t}\n\t\tif data, err := json.Marshal(auditEvent); err == nil {\n\t\t\tpal.output.Write(append(data, '\\n'))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel updates the minimum log level for policy audit events.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(logLevel logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\tpal.logLevel = logLevel\n}\n\n// SetOutput updates the custom output writer for audit logs.\n// Pass nil to disable custom output writing.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetOutput(output io.Writer) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\tpal.output = output\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1494,"cache_read_input_tokens":62343,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1494},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"39de4b3f-d86f-41c5-897e-2ab1eae45fe1","uuid":"9f9d9e3e-8eca-41d3-981c-fbbf29d6cf07"}

reason: a string explaining why this verdict was reached\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy, verdict, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity,\n\t\t\"policy\":           policy,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          verdict,\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t})\n\n\tscopedLog.Log(pal.logLevel, \"Policy decision\")\n\n\t// Write to custom output if configured\n\tif pal.output != nil {\n\t\tauditEvent := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"type\":     \"policy_decision\",\n\t\t\t\"identity\": identity,\n\t\t\t\"policy\":   policy,\n\t\t\t\"verdict\":  verdict,\n\t\t\t\"reason\":   reason,\n\t\t}\n\t\tif data, err := json.Marshal(auditEvent); err == nil {\n\t\t\tpal.output.Write(append(data, '\\n'))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs the result of a policy evaluation.\n//\n// Parameters:\n//   -
